<h3>Mapping</h3>
<a href="https://usegalaxy.eu/root?tool_id=megablast_xml_parser" title=""><button type="button" class="btn btn-outline-primary btn-rounded waves-effect btn-xs" style="margin: 2px">Parse blast XML output</button></a>
